<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管很多研究关注刻板印象或代表性偏见，但鲜有研究探讨不同身份背景用户在LLM生成回答核心质量上的差异。作者发现，即便模型知识本身对各身份稳定，实际输出却因偏置生成行为导致质量下降，这种核心质量的分化会带来严重公正性问题。

Method: 作者提出了一种无需微调训练的生成框架，可以在生成过程中有选择性地中和或隐藏对结果无关的身份信息，仅保留与语义密切相关的属性，从而减少身份对生成质量的影响。该方法通过提示工程处理，对生成内容的身份敏感部分进行再加工。

Result: 在四个基准任务和18个人口统计身份测试中，该框架相较直接（vanilla）提示法，减少了77%的身份相关偏差；相较已有的防御性提示法，也减少了45%的偏差。模型生成的核心质量和内容完整性均得以保持。

Conclusion: 该研究系统性揭示了身份信息对LLM输出质量的不公平影响，并提出了有效且易于应用的解决方法，为实现身份无关的LLM输出质量迈出了关键一步，有助于提升模型的公正性和实用性。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) outputs often vary across user sociodemographic attributes, leading to disparities in factual accuracy, utility, and safety, even for objective questions where demographic information is irrelevant. Unlike prior work on stereotypical or representational bias, this paper studies identity-dependent degradation of core response quality. We show empirically that such degradation arises from biased generation behavior, despite factual knowledge being robustly encoded across identities. Motivated by this mismatch, we propose a lightweight, training-free framework for identity-robust generation that selectively neutralizes non-critical identity information while preserving semantically essential attributes, thus maintaining output content integrity. Experiments across four benchmarks and 18 sociodemographic identities demonstrate an average 77% reduction in identity-dependent bias compared to vanilla prompting and a 45% reduction relative to prompt-based defenses. Our work addresses a critical gap in mitigating the impact of user identity cues in prompts on core generation quality.

*Zeqiang Wang,Xinyue Wu,Chenxi Li,Zixi Chen,Nishanth Sastry,Jon Johnson,Suparna De*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型和文本编码器驱动的社会科学类信息系统广泛使用，但全参数微调计算和能耗高，小型机构与公益机构难以承受。低秩适配（LoRA）等高效微调法虽然降低了成本，但存在几何结构缺陷，亟需提升。

Method: 作者首先分析了标准LoRA在几何上的缺点，如规范自由度、尺度歧义和秩坍缩。为此提出OrthoGeoLoRA，将低秩因子正交化（约束在Stiefel流形上），并采用几何重参数化实现这一约束，可直接用于现有优化器和微调流程。同时建立了社会科学层级检索新基准。

Result: 在ELSST多语种句子编码检索任务中，OrthoGeoLoRA在相同低秩预算下，在排名指标上优于标准LoRA及多个先进高效微调方法。

Conclusion: OrthoGeoLoRA为资源受限环境中的基础模型适配提供了更高效的计算与参数利用方式，尤其适合Web4Good等公益与小型组织领域。

Abstract: Large language models and text encoders increasingly power web-based information systems in the social sciences, including digital libraries, data catalogues, and search interfaces used by researchers, policymakers, and civil society. Full fine-tuning is often computationally and energy intensive, which can be prohibitive for smaller institutions and non-profit organizations in the Web4Good ecosystem. Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT), especially Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), reduces this cost by updating only a small number of parameters. We show that the standard LoRA update $ΔW = BA^\top$ has geometric drawbacks: gauge freedom, scale ambiguity, and a tendency toward rank collapse. We introduce OrthoGeoLoRA, which enforces an SVD-like form $ΔW = BΣA^\top$ by constraining the low-rank factors to be orthogonal (Stiefel manifold). A geometric reparameterization implements this constraint while remaining compatible with standard optimizers such as Adam and existing fine-tuning pipelines. We also propose a benchmark for hierarchical concept retrieval over the European Language Social Science Thesaurus (ELSST), widely used to organize social science resources in digital repositories. Experiments with a multilingual sentence encoder show that OrthoGeoLoRA outperforms standard LoRA and several strong PEFT variants on ranking metrics under the same low-rank budget, offering a more compute- and parameter-efficient path to adapt foundation models in resource-constrained settings.

### [119] [ProFit: Leveraging High-Value Signals in SFT via Probability-Guided Token Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09195)
*Tao Liu,Taiqiang Wu,Runming Yang,Shaoning Sun,Junjie Wang,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为ProFit的新方法，通过有选择地掩盖低概率词，减轻了大语言模型在单一参考答案监督微调中的表层过拟合问题，有效提升了模型的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统SFT只用单一的参考答案进行对齐，容易导致模型对非核心表述的过拟合。而大规模收集多参考答案的数据和计算成本较高，因此需要更高效的方式缓解过拟合问题。

Method: 作者通过实证分析，发现高概率词代表核心逻辑，低概率词多为可替换表达。据此，提出ProFit方法：在微调时有选择地掩盖低概率词，把训练重心偏向于核心语义，减少模型对表层表达的依赖。

Result: 大量实验证明，ProFit方法在通用推理和数学基准测试上，相较传统SFT方法具有更优表现。

Conclusion: ProFit提供了一种简单又有效的途径，缓解了单参考答案导致的过拟合，提升了大语言模型理解和生成多样化表达的能力。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) is a fundamental post-training strategy to align Large Language Models (LLMs) with human intent. However, traditional SFT often ignores the one-to-many nature of language by forcing alignment with a single reference answer, leading to the model overfitting to non-core expressions. Although our empirical analysis suggests that introducing multiple reference answers can mitigate this issue, the prohibitive data and computational costs necessitate a strategic shift: prioritizing the mitigation of single-reference overfitting over the costly pursuit of answer diversity. To achieve this, we reveal the intrinsic connection between token probability and semantic importance: high-probability tokens carry the core logical framework, while low-probability tokens are mostly replaceable expressions. Based on this insight, we propose ProFit, which selectively masks low-probability tokens to prevent surface-level overfitting. Extensive experiments confirm that ProFit consistently outperforms traditional SFT baselines on general reasoning and mathematical benchmarks.

Designed to bridge the gap between reasoning capability and inference efficiency, A.X K1 supports explicitly controllable reasoning to facilitate scalable deployment across diverse real-world scenarios. Ca2KG integrates counterfactual prompting, which exposes retrieval-dependent uncertainties in knowledge quality and reasoning reliability, with a panel-based re-scoring mechanism that stabilises predictions across interventions. Method: 提出TeachPro多标签学习框架，系统评估五大教学维度。方法包括：（1）维度锚定证据编码器，利用预训练文本编码器、可学习提示模块、交叉注意力机制，将证据与教学维度对齐；（2）跨视图图网络，包括句法分支（语法解析）和语义分支（BERT语义关联），通过BiAffine融合和差异正则促进互补表达；（3）最终用交叉注意力机制将证据与多视图评论表示结合。并构建了含专家注释和多标签分数的新基准数据集。

Result: TeachPro在多个评测设定下表现出优越的诊断粒度和稳健性，效果超过现有方法。

Conclusion: TeachPro能够系统细致地评估教学的多个关键维度，为教学反馈和改进提供更具洞察力和实用价值的分析结果。

Abstract: Standardized Student Evaluation of Teaching often suffer from low reliability, restricted response options, and response distortion. Existing machine learning methods that mine open-ended comments usually reduce feedback to binary sentiment, which overlooks concrete concerns such as content clarity, feedback timeliness, and instructor demeanor, and provides limited guidance for instructional improvement.We propose TeachPro, a multi-label learning framework that systematically assesses five key teaching dimensions: professional expertise, instructional behavior, pedagogical efficacy, classroom experience, and other performance metrics. We first propose a Dimension-Anchored Evidence Encoder, which integrates three core components: (i) a pre-trained text encoder that transforms qualitative feedback annotations into contextualized embeddings; (ii) a prompt module that represents five teaching dimensions as learnable semantic anchors; and (iii) a cross-attention mechanism that aligns evidence with pedagogical dimensions within a structured semantic space. We then propose a Cross-View Graph Synergy Network to represent student comments. This network comprises two components: (i) a Syntactic Branch that extracts explicit grammatical dependencies from parse trees, and (ii) a Semantic Branch that models latent conceptual relations derived from BERT-based similarity graphs. BiAffine fusion module aligns syntactic and semantic units, while a differential regularizer disentangles embeddings to encourage complementary representations. Finally, a cross-attention mechanism bridges the dimension-anchored evidence with the multi-view comment representations. We also contribute a novel benchmark dataset featuring expert qualitative annotations and multi-label scores. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TeachPro offers superior diagnostic granularity and robustness across diverse evaluation settings.

</details>

### [126] [ReGraM: Region-First Knowledge Graph Reasoning for Medical Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09280)
*Chaerin Lee,Sohee Park,Hyunsik Na,Daseon Choi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReGraM方法，通过在知识图谱中构建与查询对齐的子图区域，并采用分步推理，从而提升医学问答的准确性和稳定性，相较于传统全量遍历或大规模检索更有效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医学问答方法在结合大语言模型与生物医学知识图谱时，依赖全图遍历或大规模检索，这带来较多噪声和不稳定的多跳推理。作者认为核心问题不在于获取更多知识，而是找到并聚焦于与每个查询最相关的证据子集。

Method: 提出了ReGraM框架，通过针对每个查询构建对齐的局部子图，并在此区域内采用多种证据感知模式进行分步推理。该方法仅关注与问题高度相关的知识区域，避免了全图处理的不足。

Result: 在七个医学问答基准上，ReGraM相较于强基线KGARevision有显著提升：MCQ准确率提升8.04%，SAQ提升4.50%，幻觉率降低42.9%。消融和定性分析表明，区域构建与逐跳推理的结合是性能提升的主要驱动力。

Conclusion: 区域优先的知识图谱推理为医学问答带来了更高的事实性准确率与一致性，是较以往全图推理更有效的范式。

Abstract: Recent studies in medical question answering (Medical QA) have actively explored the integration of large language models (LLMs) with biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) to improve factual accuracy. However, most existing approaches still rely on traversing the entire KG or performing large-scale retrieval, which introduces substantial noise and leads to unstable multi-hop reasoning. We argue that the core challenge lies not in expanding access to knowledge, but in identifying and reasoning over the appropriate subset of evidence for each query. ReGraM is a region-first knowledge graph reasoning framework that addresses this challenge by constructing a query-aligned subgraph and performing stepwise reasoning constrained to this localized region under multiple evidence aware modes. By focusing inference on only the most relevant portion of the KG, ReGraM departs from the assumption that all relations are equally useful an assumption that rarely holds in domain-specific medical settings. Experiments on seven medical QA benchmarks demonstrate that ReGraM consistently outperforms a strong baseline (KGARevion), achieving an 8.04% absolute accuracy gain on MCQ, a 4.50% gain on SAQ, and a 42.9% reduction in hallucination rate. Ablation and qualitative analyses further show that aligning region construction with hop-wise reasoning is the primary driver of these improvements. Overall, our results highlight region-first KG reasoning as an effective paradigm for improving factual accuracy and consistency in medical QA.

### [127] [Understanding or Memorizing? A Case Study of German Definite Articles in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09313)
*Jonathan Drechsel,Erisa Bytyqi,Steffen Herbold*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言模型在处理德语定冠词语法一致性时，是否基于规则泛化还是记忆。通过解释性方法GRADIEND，发现模型倾向于依赖部分记忆关联，而非完全基于抽象语法规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然语言模型在语法一致性任务（如德语定冠词的性和格）上表现良好，但尚不清楚其是否真正学会了规则化泛化，还是只是在记忆特定模式。作者希望探究模型内部机制。

Method: 采用GRADIEND（一种基于梯度的解释性方法），学习对特定性-格组合的定冠词变换的参数更新方向，并分析这些更新对其他组合的影响及受影响神经元的重叠情况。

Result: 针对某一性-格组合学习的参数更新，往往会影响到其他无关的性-格组合，并且受影响神经元在不同设置间高度重叠。

Conclusion: 以上现象说明，语言模型在处理德语定冠词时，并非完全基于抽象的语法规则编码，而至少部分依赖于记忆的关联。

Abstract: Language models perform well on grammatical agreement, but it is unclear whether this reflects rule-based generalization or memorization. We study this question for German definite singular articles, whose forms depend on gender and case. Using GRADIEND, a gradient-based interpretability method, we learn parameter update directions for gender-case specific article transitions. We find that updates learned for a specific gender-case article transition frequently affect unrelated gender-case settings, with substantial overlap among the most affected neurons across settings. These results argue against a strictly rule-based encoding of German definite articles, indicating that models at least partly rely on memorized associations rather than abstract grammatical rules.

### [131] [The Imperfective Paradox in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09373)
*Bolei Ma,Yusuke Miyao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文探讨了大型语言模型（LLM）是否真正理解事件的组合语义，还是仅依赖表层概率启发式，通过分析“未完成体悖论”发现模型在处理目标导向事件时存在系统性虚构完成倾向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在自然语言理解上表现出色，但其是否能正确推理事件的时间结构和过程结果之间的逻辑关系尚不明确，尤其在涉及未完成体和完成体的逻辑推断时（即“未完成体悖论”），需要检测模型的深层语义能力。

Method: 作者构建了名为ImperfectiveNLI的诊断数据集，覆盖不同语义类别，通过评测主流开放权重的大型语言模型，并对模型内部表征进行分析。另外，尝试基于提示的干预策略，测试其对推理表现的影响。

Result: 发现主要LLM在“目标导向事件”上普遍存在“目的论偏差”，即模型倾向于误判事件已经完成（即使文本有否定信息），模型表示虽然能区分过程与结果，但最终推理决策受先验偏见影响较大。基于提示的干预可减少此类偏差，但也会引入新的误拒现象。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在事件结构和体貌上缺乏真实的结构性理解，更像是通过叙事预测而非逻辑推断作出结论，说明其逻辑推理能力和深层语义理解仍有明显不足。

Abstract: Do Large Language Models (LLMs) genuinely grasp the compositional semantics of events, or do they rely on surface-level probabilistic heuristics? We investigate the Imperfective Paradox, a logical phenomenon where the past progressive aspect entails event realization for activities (e.g., running $\to$ ran) but not for accomplishments (e.g., building $\nrightarrow$ built). We introduce ImperfectiveNLI, a diagnostic dataset designed to probe this distinction across diverse semantic classes. Evaluating state-of-the-art open-weight models, we uncover a pervasive Teleological Bias: models systematically hallucinate completion for goal-oriented events, often overriding explicit textual negation. Representational analyses show that while internal embeddings often distinguish process from result, inference decisions are dominated by strong priors about goal attainment. We further find that prompting-based interventions reduce hallucinated completions but also increase incorrect rejections of valid entailments. Our findings suggest that current LLMs lack structural aspectual awareness, operating as predictive narrative engines rather than faithful logical reasoners.

### [132] [Ability Transfer and Recovery via Modularized Parameters Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09398)
*Songyao Jin,Kun Zhou,Wenqi Li,Peng Wang,Biwei Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 大语言模型在专注某一领域或技能时容易遗忘其他能力。本文提出一种新方法，有效转移和融合不同模型的能力，实现能力恢复和融合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型进行领域或技能特定微调时，虽然能提升特定任务表现，但常常导致其它能力下降甚至遗忘（灾难性遗忘）。理解模型能力在参数中的分布，有望找到更高效且兼容的迁移方法。

Method: 通过分析不同输入（领域/语言）下模型各部分激活分布，发现与能力相关的激活主要集中在极少数通道（<5%）且彼此基本独立。基于此，提出ACT方法，通过激活差异定位关键通道，仅转移这些通道的参数，并用轻量级微调保证兼容性。

Result: 实验表明，ACT方法在多语言数学与科学推理任务中，能恢复因微调而丢失的能力，同时保留已有技能。还可将多个专长模型的能力有效融合进单一模型，且相互干扰很小。

Conclusion: 本文的通道级迁移方法，为大模型多能力整合与灾难遗忘恢复提供了新思路，且实现简单高效。相关代码和数据将开放。

Abstract: Large language models can be continually pre-trained or fine-tuned to improve performance in specific domains, languages, or skills, but this specialization often degrades other capabilities and may cause catastrophic forgetting. We investigate how abilities are distributed within LLM parameters by analyzing module activations under domain- and language-specific inputs for closely related models. Across layers and modules, we find that ability-related activations are highly concentrated in a small set of channels (typically <5\%), and these channels are largely disentangled with good sufficiency and stability. Building on these observations, we propose ACT (Activation-Guided Channel-wise Ability Transfer), which localizes ability-relevant channels via activation differences and selectively transfers only the corresponding parameters, followed by lightweight fine-tuning for compatibility. Experiments on multilingual mathematical and scientific reasoning show that ACT can recover forgotten abilities while preserving retained skills. It can also merge multiple specialized models to integrate several abilities into a single model with minimal interference. Our code and data will be publicly released.

</details>


### [133] [Structured Knowledge Representation through Contextual Pages for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09402)
*Xinze Li,Zhenghao Liu,Haidong Xin,Yukun Yan,Shuo Wang,Zheni Zeng,Sen Mei,Ge Yu,Maosong Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了PAGER，一种用于RAG的大型语言模型知识增强系统，通过组织结构化的知识页面，显著提升了模型的知识表达质量和问答准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG模型虽然能通过检索累积外部知识，但在多轮累积过程中缺乏系统化的结构，导致知识组织松散，影响最终知识表达质量。该研究旨在解决这一结构化不足问题。

Method: PAGER方法首先让大模型为问题生成结构化的认知大纲，将不同知识点分配到各自的槽位，然后针对每个槽位检索并精选相关文档，反复迭代优化，最终生成内容丰富、连贯的知识页面，作为上下文供大模型生成答案。

Result: 在多个知识密集型基准测试和多种主流骨干模型上，PAGER优于所有已知的RAG基线方法。分析显示，该方法不仅能构建高质量、高密度的信息知识表示，还能更好地消解知识冲突，并提升大模型对外部知识的利用能力。

Conclusion: PAGER为知识增强的大语言模型提供了结构化知识组织与表达的新范式，显著提高了知识整合和问答能力，在实际应用中具有广泛推广价值。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances Large Language Models (LLMs) by incorporating external knowledge. Recently, some works have incorporated iterative knowledge accumulation processes into RAG models to progressively accumulate and refine query-related knowledge, thereby constructing more comprehensive knowledge representations. However, these iterative processes often lack a coherent organizational structure, which limits the construction of more comprehensive and cohesive knowledge representations. To address this, we propose PAGER, a page-driven autonomous knowledge representation framework for RAG. PAGER first prompts an LLM to construct a structured cognitive outline for a given question, which consists of multiple slots representing a distinct knowledge aspect. Then, PAGER iteratively retrieves and refines relevant documents to populate each slot, ultimately constructing a coherent page that serves as contextual input for guiding answer generation. Experiments on multiple knowledge-intensive benchmarks and backbone models show that PAGER consistently outperforms all RAG baselines. Further analyses demonstrate that PAGER constructs higher-quality and information-dense knowledge representations, better mitigates knowledge conflicts, and enables LLMs to leverage external knowledge more effectively. All code is available at https://github.com/OpenBMB/PAGER.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型预训练模型（如BERT）训练成本极高，不便于反复实验探究和化解其偏见，因此推动更公平模型的研究变得困难。

Method: 作者提出采用名为BabyLMs的小型BERT变体，这些模型在小型、可控语料上训练，用于代理分析偏见形成机制和测试去偏方法，同时对比其与标准BERT模型在偏见和性能演化上的一致性。

Result: 实验表明，BabyLMs在偏见形成和性能发展上与标准BERT高度一致；它们在多种去偏方法下也呈现相似相关性。使用BabyLMs进行实验可以大幅减少实验的计算成本（GPU小时从500降至30以下），并且有效支持偏见相关的实验。

Abstract: Pre-trained language models (LMs) have, over the last few years, grown substantially in both societal adoption and training costs. This rapid growth in size has constrained progress in understanding and mitigating their biases. Since re-training LMs is prohibitively expensive, most debiasing work has focused on post-hoc or masking-based strategies, which often fail to address the underlying causes of bias. In this work, we seek to democratise pre-model debiasing research by using low-cost proxy models. Specifically, we investigate BabyLMs, compact BERT-like models trained on small and mutable corpora that can approximate bias acquisition and learning dynamics of larger models. We show that BabyLMs display closely aligned patterns of intrinsic bias formation and performance development compared to standard BERT models, despite their drastically reduced size. Furthermore, correlations between BabyLMs and BERT hold across multiple intra-model and post-model debiasing methods. Leveraging these similarities, we conduct pre-model debiasing experiments with BabyLMs, replicating prior findings and presenting new insights regarding the influence of gender imbalance and toxicity on bias formation. Our results demonstrate that BabyLMs can serve as an effective sandbox for large-scale LMs, reducing pre-training costs from over 500 GPU-hours to under 30 GPU-hours. This provides a way to democratise pre-model debiasing research and enables faster, more accessible exploration of methods for building fairer LMs.

In this work, we design a framework based on mechanistic interpretability methods to identify where and how conflicting knowledge from the pre-training data is encoded within LMs. Our findings contribute to a growing body of evidence that specific internal components of a language model are responsible for encoding conflicting knowledge from pre-training, and we demonstrate how mechanistic interpretability methods can be leveraged to causally intervene in and control conflicting knowledge at inference time.

This decomposition framework also enables the use of a verification module that targets predicate-arity errors to further improve performance. Our study evaluates three families of models across four logical-reasoning datasets. The comprehensive fine-tuning, incremental inference, and verification modules reduce error rates, increase predicate coverage, and improve reasoning performance for smaller LMs, moving us closer to developing reliable and accessible symbolic-reasoning systems.

Our code and data are available at https://github.com/YunqiaoYang/SlidesGen-Bench.

### [140] [Benchmarking Post-Training Quantization of Large Language Models under Microscaling Floating Point Formats](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09555)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者对7种PTQ算法、15个评测基准和3个LLM系列进行全面测试，主要比较了不同MXFP格式（如MXFP8和MXFP4）下PTQ算法的性能，并分析了多模态LLM中语言模型与视觉编码器对量化敏感性的影响。

Conclusion: 文章为MXFP低精度格式下的PTQ算法选择和优化提供了实证基础和操作建议，有助于提升大模型量化部署的效果。

Abstract: Microscaling Floating-Point (MXFP) has emerged as a promising low-precision format for large language models (LLMs). Despite various post-training quantization (PTQ) algorithms being proposed, they mostly focus on integer quantization, while their applicability and behavior under MXFP formats remain largely unexplored. To address this gap, this work conducts a systematic investigation of PTQ under MXFP formats, encompassing over 7 PTQ algorithms, 15 evaluation benchmarks, and 3 LLM families. The key findings include: 1) MXFP8 consistently achieves near-lossless performance, while MXFP4 introduces substantial accuracy degradation and remains challenging; 2) PTQ effectiveness under MXFP depends strongly on format compatibility, with some algorithmic paradigms being consistently more effective than others; 3) PTQ performance exhibits highly consistent trends across model families and modalities, in particular, quantization sensitivity is dominated by the language model rather than the vision encoder in multimodal LLMs; 4) The scaling factor of quantization is a critical error source in MXFP4, and a simple pre-scale optimization strategy can significantly mitigate its impact. Together, these results provide practical guidance on adapting existing PTQ methods to MXFP quantization.

### [141] [Dialogue Telemetry: Turn-Level Instrumentation for Autonomous Information Gathering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09570)
*Dimitris Panagopoulos,Adolfo Perrusquia,Weisi Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了对话遥测（DT）框架，旨在为自主系统在信息收集对话中提供回合级的观测信号，以监控效率和检测无效对话。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主系统在基于架构的信息收集对话中，缺乏对数据获取效率的实时观测手段，难以及时发现并处理对话陷入低效或停滞的问题。

Method: 提出Dialogue Telemetry（DT）框架，包括进展估计器（PE）和停滞指数（SI），前者衡量剩余信息潜力，后者检测回合内无效探查趋势。SI无需具体因果诊断，即可标记低效对话。通过在受控的大模型模拟的搜索救援情境中，对方法进行验证，并将DT信号输入强化学习策略进行实验。

Conclusion: DT为自主系统提供了通用、可解释的回合级监控指标，能提升信息收集对话的效率与策略表现。

Abstract: Autonomous systems conducting schema-grounded information-gathering dialogues face an instrumentation gap, lacking turn-level observables for monitoring acquisition efficiency and detecting when questioning becomes unproductive. We introduce Dialogue Telemetry (DT), a measurement framework that produces two model-agnostic signals after each question-answer exchange: (i) a Progress Estimator (PE) quantifying residual information potential per category (with a bits-based variant), and (ii) a Stalling Index (SI) detecting an observable failure signature characterized by repeated category probing with semantically similar, low-marginal-gain responses. SI flags this pattern without requiring causal diagnosis, supporting monitoring in settings where attributing degradation to specific causes may be impractical. We validate DT in controlled search-and-rescue (SAR)-inspired interviews using large language model (LLM)-based simulations, distinguishing efficient from stalled dialogue traces and illustrating downstream utility by integrating DT signals into a reinforcement learning (RL) policy. Across these settings, DT provides interpretable turn-level instrumentation that improves policy performance when stalling carries operational costs.

*Qian Cao,Yahui Liu,Wei Bi,Yi Zhao,Ruihua Song,Xiting Wang,Ruiming Tang,Guorui Zhou,Han Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于RL的新方法，通过引入多样性规划机制提升大型语言模型输出的多样性，并且在创意写作任务上取得了优于现有方法的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前用强化学习优化大语言模型时，往往过分追求任务性能，导致输出内容趋于单一，尤其在需要多样性和创造性的任务（如写作）中限制了模型的表现。因此，探索能够提升多样性的RL方法成为关键问题。

Method: 本文设计了一套新的RL框架。在生成过程中，将任务分解为半结构化的长链式思维（CoT）步骤，通过“多样性规划分支”(Diverse Planning Branching)方法，在规划阶段根据多样性动态调整分支，引导模型产生不同的生成路径。同时，设计了群体感知的多样性奖励(group-aware diversity reward)，全程鼓励输出内容的差异化。

Result: 在创意写作基准测试中，新方法在提升生成多样性的同时，没有损失文本的质量，在各项指标上均优于主流的现有基线方法。

Conclusion: 通过在RL框架中嵌入多样性导向的机制，能够显著提升大语言模型在开放式生成任务中的多样性表现，为相关领域提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL)-based enhancement of large language models (LLMs) often leads to reduced output diversity, undermining their utility in open-ended tasks like creative writing. Current methods lack explicit mechanisms for guiding diverse exploration and instead prioritize optimization efficiency and performance over diversity. This paper proposes an RL framework structured around a semi-structured long Chain-of-Thought (CoT), in which the generation process is decomposed into explicitly planned intermediate steps. We introduce a Diverse Planning Branching method that strategically introduces divergence at the planning phase based on diversity variation, alongside a group-aware diversity reward to encourage distinct trajectories. Experimental results on creative writing benchmarks demonstrate that our approach significantly improves output diversity without compromising generation quality, consistently outperforming existing baselines.

</details>


### [143] [LLMs Got Rhythm? Hybrid Phonological Filtering for Greek Poetry Rhyme Detection and Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09631)
*Stergios Chatzikyriakidis*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出用大型语言模型(LLMs)结合确定性语音算法，以更准确地实现希腊语诗歌押韵分析与生成，显著提升自动化押韵能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管LLM在NLP领域能力突出，但在基于音系的任务（如韵律检测和生成）表现欠佳，尤其在低资源语言（如现代希腊语）中更明显。现有模型生成押韵诗歌的准确率极低，因此亟需新的技术突破来提升其音韵识别和生成能力。

Method: 作者设计了一套混合系统，将LLMs与确定性的音韵算法结合，并实现了详细的希腊语韵律分类体系。系统用代理式生成流程，并辅以音系验证机制；对比评估了多种Prompt策略（零样本、少样本、思维链和RAG增强），并测试了多款主流LLM（如Claude 3.7/4.5，GPT-4o等）。

Result: 同为LLM模型，不同Prompt下表现差异极大。类母语模型（Claude 3.7）韵律识别准确率约40%，推理能力更强模型（Claude 4.5）通过思维链Prompt可达54%；直接生成有效诗歌极低（<4%），合成混合系统后，准确率提升至73.1%。

Conclusion: 单纯LLM在低资源语言的音韵诗歌生成任务上表现较差，通过混合音系算法显著增强了性能。作者还公开了系统及4万多条高质量希腊诗歌韵律数据集，为该领域后续研究打下基础。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs), despite their remarkable capabilities across NLP tasks, struggle with phonologically-grounded phenomena like rhyme detection and generation. This is even more evident in lower-resource languages such as Modern Greek. In this paper, we present a hybrid system that combines LLMs with deterministic phonological algorithms to achieve accurate rhyme identification/analysis and generation. Our approach implements a comprehensive taxonomy of Greek rhyme types, including Pure, Rich, Imperfect, Mosaic, and Identical Pre-rhyme Vowel (IDV) patterns, and employs an agentic generation pipeline with phonological verification. We evaluate multiple prompting strategies (zero-shot, few-shot, Chain-of-Thought, and RAG-augmented) across several LLMs including Claude 3.7 and 4.5, GPT-4o, Gemini 2.0 and open-weight models like Llama 3.1 8B and 70B and Mistral Large. Results reveal a significant "Reasoning Gap": while native-like models (Claude 3.7) perform intuitively (40\% accuracy in identification), reasoning-heavy models (Claude 4.5) achieve state-of-the-art performance (54\%) only when prompted with Chain-of-Thought. Most critically, pure LLM generation fails catastrophically (under 4\% valid poems), while our hybrid verification loop restores performance to 73.1\%. We release our system and a crucial, rigorously cleaned corpus of 40,000+ rhymes, derived from the Anemoskala and Interwar Poetry corpora, to support future research.

</details>


### [144] [TaxoBell: Gaussian Box Embeddings for Self-Supervised Taxonomy Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09633)
*Sahil Mishra,Srinitish Srinivasan,Srikanta Bedathur,Tanmoy Chakraborty*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种新的用于自动扩展分类体系（taxonomy）的嵌入方法TaxoBell，有效提升了自动分类体系构建的表现，并显著优于现有主流方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动分类体系扩展方法多采用点状向量嵌入，无法很好地模拟分类体系中的非对称“is-a”关系。盒子嵌入虽有潜力，但存在梯度不稳定、缺乏语义不确定性刻画以及难以表示歧义等问题，因此亟需更优的结构化表示方法。

Method: 提出TaxoBell方法，将box嵌入和多元高斯分布结合，通过能量函数优化，将box作为语义位置均值，协方差作为语义不确定性，有效支持不确定性表达、歧义能力和稳定优化。

Result: 在五个基准数据集上，TaxoBell在MRR提升了19%，Recall@k提升约25%，超过了八个最先进基线方法。论文还通过消融实验和错误分析详细说明了方法的优劣。

Conclusion: TaxoBell在表达分类体系结构和处理复杂语义关系方面优于现有自动方法，是taxonomy扩展问题的有效解决方案。

Abstract: Taxonomies form the backbone of structured knowledge representation across diverse domains, enabling applications such as e-commerce catalogs, semantic search, and biomedical discovery. Yet, manual taxonomy expansion is labor-intensive and cannot keep pace with the emergence of new concepts. Existing automated methods rely on point-based vector embeddings, which model symmetric similarity and thus struggle with the asymmetric "is-a" relationships that are fundamental to taxonomies. Box embeddings offer a promising alternative by enabling containment and disjointness, but they face key issues: (i) unstable gradients at the intersection boundaries, (ii) no notion of semantic uncertainty, and (iii) limited capacity to represent polysemy or ambiguity. We address these shortcomings with TaxoBell, a Gaussian box embedding framework that translates between box geometries and multivariate Gaussian distributions, where means encode semantic location and covariances encode uncertainty. Energy-based optimization yields stable optimization, robust modeling of ambiguous concepts, and interpretable hierarchical reasoning. Extensive experimentation on five benchmark datasets demonstrates that TaxoBell significantly outperforms eight state-of-the-art taxonomy expansion baselines by 19% in MRR and around 25% in Recall@k. We further demonstrate the advantages and pitfalls of TaxoBell with error analysis and ablation studies.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在五种语言、五个数据集（含新构建的中文数据集）上对USAS基于规则的系统进行最大范围评测，同时新标注英文训练集，训练并测试多种单语/跨语神经模型，并和规则方法对比，探索二者融合途径。

Result: USAS规则系统在多语种场景下性能得到详细测评，神经网络模型在多数据集上表现良好，融合模型进一步提升了系统表现。所有模型、数据和代码实现已公开。

Conclusion: 神经网络方法可有效增强USAS的规则系统，推动多语言、跨语言的语义分析工具发展，开源资源也促进了今后相关研究。

Abstract: Word Sense Disambiguation (WSD) has been widely evaluated using the semantic frameworks of WordNet, BabelNet, and the Oxford Dictionary of English. However, for the UCREL Semantic Analysis System (USAS) framework, no open extensive evaluation has been performed beyond lexical coverage or single language evaluation. In this work, we perform the largest semantic tagging evaluation of the rule based system that uses the lexical resources in the USAS framework covering five different languages using four existing datasets and one novel Chinese dataset. We create a new silver labelled English dataset, to overcome the lack of manually tagged training data, that we train and evaluate various mono and multilingual neural models in both mono and cross-lingual evaluation setups with comparisons to their rule based counterparts, and show how a rule based system can be enhanced with a neural network model. The resulting neural network models, including the data they were trained on, the Chinese evaluation dataset, and all of the code have been released as open resources.

</details>


### [146] [DeepResearchEval: An Automated Framework for Deep Research Task Construction and Agentic Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09688)
*Yibo Wang,Lei Wang,Yue Deng,Keming Wu,Yao Xiao,Huanjin Yao,Liwei Kang,Hai Ye,Yongcheng Jing,Lidong Bing*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了DeepResearchEval，这是一个自动化的深度研究任务构建与智能评估框架，能够生成多元复杂的研究任务，并自动、动态地评估深度研究系统的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前深度研究系统的评估存在诸多挑战，如任务构建需大量人工标注、评价维度静态且难以适应任务差异，以及在缺少引用时事实核查不可靠。现有基准存在局限，急需更高效和智能的评测工具。

Method: 作者提出了两个主要方法：1）任务构建采用基于人物画像的流程，生成多样复杂的仿真研究任务，并通过“两阶段筛选”机制压缩到真正需要多源证据整合和外部检索支持的任务；2）评估部分设计了智能评价管线，包括可自适应的“逐点质量评价”，动态确定评价维度、标准和权重，以及主动事实核查，即便缺乏明确引用也能从网络自动核查并验证文中陈述。

Result: DeepResearchEval能够实现自动化、多任务个性化的评估流程，成功生成高质量复杂任务，并能够动态且有效地评价和核查深度研究系统的输出，减少人工工作量，提高真实性和公平性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的DeepResearchEval为深度研究系统评估提供了创新、高效的自动化解决方案，大幅提升了任务复杂性、评估针对性和核查能力，为未来的深度研究自动化和大模型评测奠定了基础。

Abstract: Deep research systems are widely used for multi-step web research, analysis, and cross-source synthesis, yet their evaluation remains challenging. Existing benchmarks often require annotation-intensive task construction, rely on static evaluation dimensions, or fail to reliably verify facts when citations are missing. To bridge these gaps, we introduce DeepResearchEval, an automated framework for deep research task construction and agentic evaluation. For task construction, we propose a persona-driven pipeline generating realistic, complex research tasks anchored in diverse user profiles, applying a two-stage filter Task Qualification and Search Necessity to retain only tasks requiring multi-source evidence integration and external retrieval. For evaluation, we propose an agentic pipeline with two components: an Adaptive Point-wise Quality Evaluation that dynamically derives task-specific evaluation dimensions, criteria, and weights conditioned on each generated task, and an Active Fact-Checking that autonomously extracts and verifies report statements via web search, even when citations are missing.

### [147] [Routing with Generated Data: Annotation-Free LLM Skill Estimation and Expert Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09692)
*Tianyi Niu,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Genta Indra Winata,Shi-Xiong Zhang,Supriyo Chakraborty,Sambit Sahu,Yue Zhang,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种只用大语言模型自动生成的数据训练路由器的方法，并引入了CASCAL，一个更加鲁棒且无需答案的路由算法，在弱生成器数据下也有明显精度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实中，手动标注真实标签的数据很稀缺，特别是当用户请求分布异质且未知时，依赖真值数据训练路由器不现实，因此需要研究能仅凭生成数据有效训练的路由方案。

Method: 论文提出Routing with Generated Data (RGD) 设定，只利用由生成型大语言模型基于高层任务描述自动生成的问答数据，分别评估了“查询-答案路由器”和“仅查询路由器”。分析发现，生成器需要准确自答且其问题要能区分模型性能。为此，作者设计数据筛选策略并提出新的CASCAL算法，通过共识投票和层次聚类，估计模型正确性并识别模型专长领域。

Result: 在4个基准任务和12个模型上实验显示，随着生成器质量下降，查询-答案路由器性能衰减更快；CASCAL作为仅查询路由器，在生成器较弱时比最佳查询-答案路由器高4.6%绝对精度。

Conclusion: 利用精心筛选的自动生成数据和新路由算法CASCAL，可以在无真实标签场景下，多模型系统实现更高的路由精度和更强的生成器鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) routers dynamically select optimal models for given inputs. Existing approaches typically assume access to ground-truth labeled data, which is often unavailable in practice, especially when user request distributions are heterogeneous and unknown. We introduce Routing with Generated Data (RGD), a challenging setting in which routers are trained exclusively on generated queries and answers produced from high-level task descriptions by generator LLMs. We evaluate query-answer routers (using both queries and labels) and query-only routers across four diverse benchmarks and 12 models, finding that query-answer routers degrade faster than query-only routers as generator quality decreases. Our analysis reveals two crucial characteristics of effective generators: they must accurately respond to their own questions, and their questions must produce sufficient performance differentiation among the model pool. We then show how filtering for these characteristics can improve the quality of generated data. We further propose CASCAL, a novel query-only router that estimates model correctness through consensus voting and identifies model-specific skill niches via hierarchical clustering. CASCAL is substantially more robust to generator quality, outperforming the best query-answer router by 4.6% absolute accuracy when trained on weak generator data.

### [148] [LLMs can Compress LLMs: Adaptive Pruning by Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09694)
*Sai Varun Kodathala,Rakesh Vunnam*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由基础模型引导（agent-guided）的剪枝方法，通过智能选择每层的剪枝操作，有效保留大模型的关键信息，在不需要重新训练的前提下大幅提升剪枝性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型剪枝方法要么依赖经验性规则决定各层稀疏率，要么导致模型事实知识记忆力严重退化。因此需要一种智能且泛化更强的方法来进行更优的剪枝。

Method: 提出agent-guided pruning方法，将基础语言模型作为剪枝agent，结合激活、权重和梯度重要性统计生成灵敏度剖面，由LLM agent融合自反能力进行剪枝策略调整，并设有回滚机制防止性能退化。无需重新训练，且方法模型无关。

Result: 在约45%稀疏率下，对Qwen3 4B和8B模型实验：MMLU准确率提升56%，FreebaseQA事实记忆提升19倍，困惑度下降69%。修正与自适应效果显著，平均仅需2-4次回滚，显著优于以往结构化剪枝方法。

Conclusion: 基础模型可作为智能agent指导其它基础模型压缩，实现高效知识保留和性能维持，方法无需重训练且具备广泛适用性。

Abstract: As Large Language Models (LLMs) continue to scale, post-training pruning has emerged as a promising approach to reduce computational costs while preserving performance. Existing methods such as SparseGPT and Wanda achieve high sparsity through layer-wise weight reconstruction or activation-aware magnitude pruning, but rely on uniform or hand-crafted heuristics to determine per-layer sparsity ratios. Moreover, recent work has shown that pruned LLMs suffer from severe factual knowledge degradation, with structured pruning methods experiencing near-total collapse in factual question-answering capabilities. We introduce agent-guided pruning, where a foundation model acts as an adaptive pruning agent to intelligently select which layers to prune at each iteration while preserving critical knowledge pathways. Our method constructs layer-wise sensitivity profiles by combining Wanda-inspired weight-activation metrics with gradient importance scores, normalized as z-scores for model-agnostic comparison. These statistics are processed by an LLM agent equipped with self-reflection capabilities, enabling it to learn from previous pruning outcomes and iteratively refine its strategy. A checkpoint rollback mechanism maintains model quality by reverting when perplexity degradation exceeds a threshold. We evaluate our approach on Qwen3 models (4B and 8B parameters) at approximately 45% sparsity, demonstrating substantial improvements over structured pruning baselines: 56% relative improvement in MMLU accuracy, 19x better factual knowledge retention on FreebaseQA, and 69% lower perplexity degradation. Notably, our framework requires no retraining, operates in a model-agnostic manner, and exhibits effective self-correction with only 2-4 rollbacks across 21-40 iterations, demonstrating that foundation models can effectively guide the compression of other foundation models.

</details>


### [149] [Empathy Applicability Modeling for General Health Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09696)
*Shan Randhawa,Agha Ali Raza,Kentaro Toyama,Julie Hui,Mustafa Naseem*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种理论驱动的新框架（EAF），用于在LLM参与的医疗场景中预测患者咨询中是否需要同理心。“同理心适用性”可在回复生成前被识别。研究还发布了相关基准数据，并验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在医疗领域，医生与患者高质量沟通尤其依赖同理心表达。目前NLP方法多数只是对医生回答是否同理心进行标注，无法主动预测哪些患者问题需要情感关怀。尤其是在一般性健康咨询中，现有方法对同理心需求的前瞻建模能力明显不足。

Method: 作者提出Empathy Applicability Framework（EAF），依据临床、语境与语言线索将患者问题分为是否需情感反应或解释，并构建了含有真人与GPT-4o双重标注的真实患者问题数据集。然后用人类标注和GPT标注分别训练分类器，预测“同理心适用性”，并与基于启发式和LLM零样本方法做对比。

Result: 在人类一致标注子集上，GPT与人类意见高度一致。用EAF训练的分类器预测同理心需求表现优异，超过零样本和启发式基线。误差分析发现隐性痛苦、临床严重性模糊及语境困境仍是挑战。

Conclusion: EAF首次为异步医疗场景实现了主动、前瞻式同理心需求识别，建立了相关任务基准并提升了同理心交互支持。也指出后续需多标注者、临床人员参与调优及文化多元数据。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly being integrated into clinical workflows, yet they often lack clinical empathy, an essential aspect of effective doctor-patient communication. Existing NLP frameworks focus on reactively labeling empathy in doctors' responses but offer limited support for anticipatory modeling of empathy needs, especially in general health queries. We introduce the Empathy Applicability Framework (EAF), a theory-driven approach that classifies patient queries in terms of the applicability of emotional reactions and interpretations, based on clinical, contextual, and linguistic cues. We release a benchmark of real patient queries, dual-annotated by Humans and GPT-4o. In the subset with human consensus, we also observe substantial human-GPT alignment. To validate EAF, we train classifiers on human-labeled and GPT-only annotations to predict empathy applicability, achieving strong performance and outperforming the heuristic and zero-shot LLM baselines. Error analysis highlights persistent challenges: implicit distress, clinical-severity ambiguity, and contextual hardship, underscoring the need for multi-annotator modeling, clinician-in-the-loop calibration, and culturally diverse annotation. EAF provides a framework for identifying empathy needs before response generation, establishes a benchmark for anticipatory empathy modeling, and enables supporting empathetic communication in asynchronous healthcare.

</details>


### [150] [Value-Aware Numerical Representations for Transformer Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09706)
*Andreea Dutulescu,Stefan Ruseti,Mihai Dascalu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进Transformer语言模型数值处理能力的方法，通过为数字输入添加基于数值的特殊前缀token，使模型对数值及其大小更加敏感，从而提升算术任务表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的语言模型虽然在数学推理任务上表现优秀，但在基本的数值理解和算术计算上易犯系统性错误，主要原因是阿拉伯数字被当作普通符号token处理，模型嵌入层未显式编码其实际“数值”。

Method: 作者提出为每个数字输入增加一个前缀token，该token的嵌入根据具体数值进行条件化。这样方法无需修改原有分词器和解码Transformer架构，同时在输入空间直接注入数值大小信息。

Result: 在多种数字格式、任务类型和操作数长度下，本文方法在算术任务中均优于传统baseline模型。

Conclusion: 在输入层显式编码数值信息是一种简单高效的提升语言模型数值鲁棒性的方法。

Abstract: Transformer-based language models often achieve strong results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks while remaining fragile on basic numerical understanding and arithmetic operations. A central limitation is that numbers are processed as symbolic tokens whose embeddings do not explicitly encode numerical value, leading to systematic errors. We introduce a value-aware numerical representation that augments standard tokenized inputs with a dedicated prefix token whose embedding is explicitly conditioned on the underlying numerical value. This mechanism injects magnitude information directly into the model's input space while remaining compatible with existing tokenizers and decoder-only Transformer architectures. Evaluation on arithmetic tasks shows that the proposed approach outperforms baselines across numerical formats, tasks, and operand lengths. These results indicate that explicitly encoding numerical value is an effective and efficient way to improve fundamental numerical robustness in language models.

</details>

### [151] [Fairness risk and its privacy-enabled solution in AI-driven robotic applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.08953)
*Le Liu,Bangguo Yu,Nynke Vellinga,Ming Cao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文关注生成式AI在自主机器人决策中的公平性与隐私问题，提出了兼顾用户效用的新公平度量方法，并发现隐私预算可用作实现公平性的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI逐渐成为未来社会复杂决策的核心引擎，但相关应用在公平性方面存在重大隐患，尤其在机器人系统中，缺乏能量化用户效用和考虑数据随机性的可操作公平定义。

Method: 作者提出了一个基于用户效用的公平度量标准，通过理论分析，将公平性与用户数据隐私联系起来，推导出隐私预算对公平度量的调控条件，并在机器人导航任务上进行实验验证。

Result: 发现大多数需要合规的机器人系统会强制执行用户隐私，而隐私预算实际上可被用来同时实现公平目标，即在保护隐私的同时还能达成期望的公平性。

Conclusion: 通过将公平性与隐私预算结合进行系统性考量，本文为AI伦理与自主机器人部署提供了新的理论和实践基础，有助于增强社会对AI系统的信任。

Abstract: Complex decision-making by autonomous machines and algorithms could underpin the foundations of future society. Generative AI is emerging as a powerful engine for such transitions. However, we show that Generative AI-driven developments pose a critical pitfall: fairness concerns. In robotic applications, although intuitions about fairness are common, a precise and implementable definition that captures user utility and inherent data randomness is missing. Here we provide a utility-aware fairness metric for robotic decision making and analyze fairness jointly with user-data privacy, deriving conditions under which privacy budgets govern fairness metrics. This yields a unified framework that formalizes and quantifies fairness and its interplay with privacy, which is tested in a robot navigation task. In view of the fact that under legal requirements, most robotic systems will enforce user privacy, the approach shows surprisingly that such privacy budgets can be jointly used to meet fairness targets. Addressing fairness concerns in the creative combined consideration of privacy is a step towards ethical use of AI and strengthens trust in autonomous robots deployed in everyday environments.

</details>


### [152] [Generalizable Geometric Prior and Recurrent Spiking Feature Learning for Humanoid Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09031)
*Xuetao Li,Wenke Huang,Mang Ye,Jifeng Xuan,Bo Du,Sheng Liu,Miao Li*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的人形机器人操作方法RGMP-S，结合了多模态策略和脉冲神经网络，实现了高效、泛化的机器人技能学习和动作合成，在各类仿真和现实机器人平台上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人形机器人在执行复杂人类任务时，需要进行高层次语义推理和底层动作生成。但它们在精确场景理解及高效利用人类演示样本方面仍面临巨大挑战，这些问题严重限制了机器人操作的实际泛化能力和适用范围。

Method: 提出了RGMP-S方法，通过引入2D几何归纳偏置帮助模型基于视觉-语言理解实现精准3D场景建模，利用递归自适应脉冲网络表征机器人和物体间复杂的时空交互，防止在样本稀疏时过拟合，并通过长期几何先验技能选择器，提高语义指令与空间约束对齐，实现动作的高效泛化。

Result: 在Maniskill仿真基准和三个异构真实机器人系统上（包括自研人形机器人、桌面机械臂和商业平台）进行了大量实验，结果显示本文方法在泛化、动作合成及性能上均显著优于当前主流基线方法。

Conclusion: RGMP-S能够完成复杂的人形机器人操作任务，且在可迁移性、数据效率和泛化能力方面具备明显优势。文中方法对推进高层次语义-操作耦合与动作学习具重要参考价值，相关代码和演示已开源以便复现。

Abstract: Humanoid robot manipulation is a crucial research area for executing diverse human-level tasks, involving high-level semantic reasoning and low-level action generation. However, precise scene understanding and sample-efficient learning from human demonstrations remain critical challenges, severely hindering the applicability and generalizability of existing frameworks. This paper presents a novel RGMP-S, Recurrent Geometric-prior Multimodal Policy with Spiking features, facilitating both high-level skill reasoning and data-efficient motion synthesis. To ground high-level reasoning in physical reality, we leverage lightweight 2D geometric inductive biases to enable precise 3D scene understanding within the vision-language model. Specifically, we construct a Long-horizon Geometric Prior Skill Selector that effectively aligns the semantic instructions with spatial constraints, ultimately achieving robust generalization in unseen environments. For the data efficiency issue in robotic action generation, we introduce a Recursive Adaptive Spiking Network. We parameterize robot-object interactions via recursive spiking for spatiotemporal consistency, fully distilling long-horizon dynamic features while mitigating the overfitting issue in sparse demonstration scenarios. Extensive experiments are conducted across the Maniskill simulation benchmark and three heterogeneous real-world robotic systems, encompassing a custom-developed humanoid, a desktop manipulator, and a commercial robotic platform. Empirical results substantiate the superiority of our method over state-of-the-art baselines and validate the efficacy of the proposed modules in diverse generalization scenarios. To facilitate reproducibility, the source code and video demonstrations are publicly available at https://github.com/xtli12/RGMP-S.git.

</details>


### [153] [Design Methodology of Hydraulically-driven Soft Robotic Gripper for a Large and Heavy Object](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09104)
*Ko Yamamoto,Kyosuke Ishibashi,Hiroki Ishikawa,Osamu Azami*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于液压驱动的软体机械手，能够抓取直径20-30厘米、重量达10-20千克的大型重物，这是现有以气动为主的软体机械手无法实现的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有气动驱动的软体机械手由于压力限制，输出力有限，无法抓取大型重物。因此，亟需开发一种输出力更大的新型驱动方法，以满足实际工业或服务场景下对抓取重物的需求。

Method: 作者采用液压驱动代替气动，通过建立数学模型，分析驱动力、弯曲角度、物体质量与抓取力之间的关系，确定设计参数，并结合有限元分析优化材料选择。最终设计出符合要求的软体机械手，并进行实验验证。

Result: 实验结果表明，该液压软体机械手能够稳定抓取20千克的重物，并实现了手指弯曲角度的闭环控制。

Conclusion: 液压驱动为软体机械手抓取重物提供了有效方案。通过合理设计和材料选择，液压软体机械手具备实际应用潜力，显著扩展了软体机械手的应用场景。

Abstract: This paper presents a design methodology of a hydraulically-driven soft robotic gripper for grasping a large and heavy object -- approximately 10 - 20 kg with 20 - 30 cm diameter. Most existing soft grippers are pneumatically actuated with several hundred kPa pressure, and cannot generate output force sufficient for such a large and heavy object. Instead of pneumatic actuation, hydraulic actuation has a potential to generate much larger power by several MPa pressure. In this study, we develop a hydraulically-driven soft gripper, in which its basic design parameters are determined based on a mathematical model that represents the relationship among the driving pressure, bending angle, object mass and grasping force. Moreover, we selected materials suitable for grasping a heavier object, based on the finite element analysis result of the detailed design. We report experimental results on a 20 kg object grasping and closed-loop control of the finger bending angle.

</details>


### [154] [CEI: A Unified Interface for Cross-Embodiment Visuomotor Policy Learning in 3D Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09163)
*Tong Wu,Shoujie Li,Junhao Gong,Changqing Guo,Xingting Li,Shilong Mu,Wenbo Ding*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了Cross-Embodiment Interface（CEI），突破了当前机器人通用模型过度依赖特定视角、机械臂和夹持器的瓶颈，实现不同机器人间的操作技能迁移，显著提升泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大型操作数据集训练的机器人模型容易过拟合于特定的机器人结构和数据采集视角，导致在不同机械臂和末端执行器（如夹持器）上的泛化能力较差，限制了模型的实际应用范围。

Method: 提出Cross-Embodiment Interface（CEI）框架，核心是提出“功能相似性”概念并用Directional Chamfer Distance量化，通过梯度优化对齐不同机器人的轨迹，进而合成新型机器人（不同机械臂与末端执行器）所需的观察与动作，实现演示迁移。

Result: 在仿真环境下，CEI能将Franka Panda机器人的数据和策略迁移到16种不同机器人结构上，涵盖3项任务；在实际机器人（UR5+AG95与UR5+Xhand）中双向迁移，在6项实物任务中平均迁移率达82.4%。同时还展示了CEI在空间泛化和多模态运动生成上的扩展能力。

Conclusion: CEI显著提升了操作型机器人跨结构迁移和泛化能力，有望推动通用机器人模型在复杂多样硬件上的广泛应用。

Abstract: Robotic foundation models trained on large-scale manipulation datasets have shown promise in learning generalist policies, but they often overfit to specific viewpoints, robot arms, and especially parallel-jaw grippers due to dataset biases. To address this limitation, we propose Cross-Embodiment Interface (\CEI), a framework for cross-embodiment learning that enables the transfer of demonstrations across different robot arm and end-effector morphologies. \CEI introduces the concept of \textit{functional similarity}, which is quantified using Directional Chamfer Distance. Then it aligns robot trajectories through gradient-based optimization, followed by synthesizing observations and actions for unseen robot arms and end-effectors. In experiments, \CEI transfers data and policies from a Franka Panda robot to \textbf{16} different embodiments across \textbf{3} tasks in simulation, and supports bidirectional transfer between a UR5+AG95 gripper robot and a UR5+Xhand robot across \textbf{6} real-world tasks, achieving an average transfer ratio of 82.4\%. Finally, we demonstrate that \CEI can also be extended with spatial generalization and multimodal motion generation capabilities using our proposed techniques. Project website: https://cross-embodiment-interface.github.io/

</details>


### [155] [Vision-Conditioned Variational Bayesian Last Layer Dynamics Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09178)
*Paul Brunzema,Thomas Lew,Ray Zhang,Takeru Shirasawa,John Subosits,Marcus Greiff*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合视觉信息的动态模型，使机器人系统能提前感知环境变化并进行前瞻性适应，在车辆赛道实验中表现突出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在快速变化的环境中进行自主控制时，传统模型难以应对系统行为的突变，自适应方法又过于滞后，无法及时保障安全，因此需要一种能够基于环境变化做出提前预测和调整的控制方法。

Method: 提出了一个视觉条件化的变分贝叶斯最后一层动力学模型。该模型首先学习车辆的标称动力学，然后通过对潜在特征的仿射变换进行微调，从而实现结合视觉语境的动态预测，并将其集成进最优控制器应用于赛车控制。

Result: 在Lexus LC500赛车穿越积水路段的实验中，采用视觉条件动态模型的系统在不断变化的条件下顺利完成了全部12圈，而未集成视觉的对比系统则都失控失败。

Conclusion: 主动利用视觉信息进行动力学前瞻性适应对于高性能机器人系统的安全与稳定至关重要，所提方法显著优于传统或仅靠被动适应的方案。

Abstract: Agile control of robotic systems often requires anticipating how the environment affects system behavior. For example, a driver must perceive the road ahead to anticipate available friction and plan actions accordingly. Achieving such proactive adaptation within autonomous frameworks remains a challenge, particularly under rapidly changing conditions. Traditional modeling approaches often struggle to capture abrupt variations in system behavior, while adaptive methods are inherently reactive and may adapt too late to ensure safety. We propose a vision-conditioned variational Bayesian last-layer dynamics model that leverages visual context to anticipate changes in the environment. The model first learns nominal vehicle dynamics and is then fine-tuned with feature-wise affine transformations of latent features, enabling context-aware dynamics prediction. The resulting model is integrated into an optimal controller for vehicle racing. We validate our method on a Lexus LC500 racing through water puddles. With vision-conditioning, the system completed all 12 attempted laps under varying conditions. In contrast, all baselines without visual context consistently lost control, demonstrating the importance of proactive dynamics adaptation in high-performance applications.

</details>


### [156] [Online Trajectory Optimization for Arbitrary-Shaped Mobile Robots via Polynomial Separating Hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09231)
*Shuoye Li,Zhiyuan Song,Yulin Li,Zhihai Bi,Jun Ma*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新型轨迹优化方法，利用多项式参数化的非线性分离超曲面解决复杂环境中的避障问题，无需保守的凸近似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有避障优化方法依赖于线性分离超平面，只适用于凸集，导致在复杂或狭窄环境下近似过于保守，限制了机器人的运动能力。

Method: 作者提出用多项式函数参数化的非线性分离超曲面，同时优化轨迹和分离多项式的系数，将机器人和障碍物的碰撞避免问题转化为可由标准非线性规划求解的优化问题。理论上推广了经典分离超平面定理，证明任意两个不相交有界闭集可被多项式超曲面分离。

Result: 方法通过仿真和真实机器人实验，在非凸机器人和复杂场景下，实现了平滑、无碰撞且灵活的运动表现，相比传统凸近似方法效果更优。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法去除了凸集假设，理论和实验均表明其可高效解决任意几何形状下的避障优化问题，具有较好通用性和实用价值。

Abstract: An emerging class of trajectory optimization methods enforces collision avoidance by jointly optimizing the robot's configuration and a separating hyperplane. However, as linear separators only apply to convex sets, these methods require convex approximations of both the robot and obstacles, which becomes an overly conservative assumption in cluttered and narrow environments. In this work, we unequivocally remove this limitation by introducing nonlinear separating hypersurfaces parameterized by polynomial functions. We first generalize the classical separating hyperplane theorem and prove that any two disjoint bounded closed sets in Euclidean space can be separated by a polynomial hypersurface, serving as the theoretical foundation for nonlinear separation of arbitrary geometries. Building on this result, we formulate a nonlinear programming (NLP) problem that jointly optimizes the robot's trajectory and the coefficients of the separating polynomials, enabling geometry-aware collision avoidance without conservative convex simplifications. The optimization remains efficiently solvable using standard NLP solvers. Simulation and real-world experiments with nonconvex robots demonstrate that our method achieves smooth, collision-free, and agile maneuvers in environments where convex-approximation baselines fail.

</details>


### [157] [Feedback-Based Mobile Robot Navigation in 3-D Environments Using Artificial Potential Functions Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09318)
*Ro'i Lang,Elon Rimon*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本报告提出和分析了一种基于多项式导航函数的三维空间中的运动规划方法，能够有效避开球形和柱形障碍物，并在理论和数值上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维空间中的运动规划由于障碍物复杂分布，容易导致规划函数存在局部极小值，使得机器人陷入困境。提升导航函数的全局性和鲁棒性是三维路径规划研究的核心难点。

Method: 将工作空间建模为有界球体区域，并用平滑多项式隐式函数表示障碍物，构造多项式导航函数，提出其不存在局部极小值且唯一极小点在目标点的充分条件，同时分析了其梯度和Hessian矩阵性质。

Result: 理论分析证明了所提导航函数在存在交叠障碍物的三维空间中依然可以避免局部极小值。数值仿真结果展示了该方法在障碍物密集场景下的有效性和正确性。

Conclusion: 多项式导航函数为三维空间中的运动规划提供了解决陷入局部极小值问题的可行方案，验证了该方法在复杂障碍物环境下的实用性和可靠性。

Abstract: This technical report presents the construction and analysis of polynomial navigation functions for motion planning in 3-D workspaces populated by spherical and cylindrical obstacles. The workspace is modeled as a bounded spherical region, and obstacles are encoded using smooth polynomial implicit functions. We establish conditions under which the proposed navigation functions admit a unique non-degenerate minimum at the target while avoiding local minima, including in the presence of pairwise intersecting obstacles. Gradient and Hessian analyses are provided, and the theoretical results are validated through numerical simulations in obstacle rich 3-D environments.

</details>


### [158] [ReflexDiffusion: Reflection-Enhanced Trajectory Planning for High-lateral-acceleration Scenarios in Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09377)
*Xuemei Yao,Xiao Yang,Jianbin Sun,Liuwei Xie,Xuebin Shao,Xiyu Fang,Hang Su,Kewei Yang*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新方法ReflexDiffusion，通过反射性调整增强扩散模型在推理阶段的轨迹规划，显著提升了自动驾驶在极端侧向加速度场景下的安全性和可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在自动驾驶车辆轨迹规划中，长尾极端场景（如急转弯等高侧向加速度）通常因数据稀缺导致模型性能不佳，当前规划器在这类关键安全场景下表现出系统性失败，限制了自动驾驶安全性。

Method: 提出ReflexDiffusion：在扩散模型的推理阶段引入基于梯度的反射性调整机制。具体方法是在每次标准轨迹更新后，计算条件噪声和无条件噪声预测的梯度，以增强路况曲率和车辆动态等关键约束信号，从而实现物理约束的严格遵守，尤其提升高侧向加速度下的轨迹稳定性。

Result: 在nuPlan Test14-hard基准上，ReflexDiffusion对高侧向加速度场景的驾驶分数相较当前SOTA方法提高了14.1%。

Conclusion: 推理阶段的轨迹优化可有效弥补训练数据不足，通过动态强化安全关键约束，可直接部署于现有扩散式轨迹规划器，提高自动驾驶在极端场景下的安全性，具备良好的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Generating safe and reliable trajectories for autonomous vehicles in long-tail scenarios remains a significant challenge, particularly for high-lateral-acceleration maneuvers such as sharp turns, which represent critical safety situations. Existing trajectory planners exhibit systematic failures in these scenarios due to data imbalance. This results in insufficient modelling of vehicle dynamics, road geometry, and environmental constraints in high-risk situations, leading to suboptimal or unsafe trajectory prediction when vehicles operate near their physical limits. In this paper, we introduce ReflexDiffusion, a novel inference-stage framework that enhances diffusion-based trajectory planners through reflective adjustment. Our method introduces a gradient-based adjustment mechanism during the iterative denoising process: after each standard trajectory update, we compute the gradient between the conditional and unconditional noise predictions to explicitly amplify critical conditioning signals, including road curvature and lateral vehicle dynamics. This amplification enforces strict adherence to physical constraints, particularly improving stability during high-lateral-acceleration maneuvers where precise vehicle-road interaction is paramount. Evaluated on the nuPlan Test14-hard benchmark, ReflexDiffusion achieves a 14.1% improvement in driving score for high-lateral-acceleration scenarios over the state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods. This demonstrates that inference-time trajectory optimization can effectively compensate for training data sparsity by dynamically reinforcing safety-critical constraints near handling limits. The framework's architecture-agnostic design enables direct deployment to existing diffusion-based planners, offering a practical solution for improving autonomous vehicle safety in challenging driving conditions.

</details>


### [159] [Data Scaling for Navigation in Unknown Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09444)
*Lauri Suomela,Naoki Takahata,Sasanka Kuruppu Arachchige,Harry Edelman,Joni-Kristian Kämäräinen*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文通过大规模实地实验，分析了数据量和数据多样性对模仿学习导航策略泛化能力的影响。结果显示数据多样性比单纯数据量更关键，并展示了在未见环境下的零样本导航能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管模仿学习能在熟悉环境中有效导航，但对于未见过的新环境的泛化能力仍然很弱。作者希望找到提升泛化能力的关键因素（数据量与多样性），解决实际机器人部署面临的主要难题。

Method: 作者收集并整理了来自35个国家、161个地点、总计4565小时的众包导航数据，训练视觉导航策略，并在4个国家的自动驾驶人行道机器人上进行实地闭环测试，系统性评估不同数据规模和多样性对性能的影响。

Result: 实验显示，充足的数据能够实现未知环境下的零样本导航，性能接近专门针对环境训练的策略。最重要的是，增加数据的地理多样性比单纯增加同一地点的数据对提升泛化能力有更大益处。此外，面对有噪声的众包数据，简单的回归模型表现优于生成式和序列模型。

Conclusion: 数据多样性是提升视觉导航泛化能力的关键。未来在收集和使用导航训练数据时应优先扩大场景与地理多样性，而不是单纯追求数据总量。

Abstract: Generalization of imitation-learned navigation policies to environments unseen in training remains a major challenge. We address this by conducting the first large-scale study of how data quantity and data diversity affect real-world generalization in end-to-end, map-free visual navigation. Using a curated 4,565-hour crowd-sourced dataset collected across 161 locations in 35 countries, we train policies for point goal navigation and evaluate their closed-loop control performance on sidewalk robots operating in four countries, covering 125 km of autonomous driving.
  Our results show that large-scale training data enables zero-shot navigation in unknown environments, approaching the performance of policies trained with environment-specific demonstrations. Critically, we find that data diversity is far more important than data quantity. Doubling the number of geographical locations in a training set decreases navigation errors by ~15%, while performance benefit from adding data from existing locations saturates with very little data. We also observe that, with noisy crowd-sourced data, simple regression-based models outperform generative and sequence-based architectures. We release our policies, evaluation setup and example videos on the project page.

</details>


### [160] [CLARE: Continual Learning for Vision-Language-Action Models via Autonomous Adapter Routing and Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09512)
*Ralf Römer,Yi Zhang,Angela P. Schoellig*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新方法CLARE，实现机器人视觉-语言-动作模型（VLA）在连续学习新任务时无需保存历史数据、不依赖任务标识，并显著提升了旧知识保持能力和新任务适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器人学习复杂操作任务常通过微调预训练的VLA模型，但传统微调方式导致已学知识遗忘，不适合长期、多任务、适应性要求高的实际应用。现有机器人持续学习方法往往需要存储往期数据、难以处理长任务序列，或依赖任务标签，存在现实部署难题。

Method: 提出了CLARE框架，在VLA模型部分前馈层中引入轻量模块化adapter，仅在必要时自主扩展模型规模，并通过逐层特征相似性指导扩展位置。部署阶段利用自编码器机制实现动态路由，无需任务标签即可激活最相关adapter。完全摒弃保存历史样本，具有高参数效率。

Result: 在LIBERO基准测试中，CLARE对新任务适应强，并能有效避免灾难性遗忘，整体性能明显优于包括基于样本回放的主流方法。

Conclusion: CLARE能实现高效、泛化性强的无样本持续学习，提升机器人长期自适应能力，在实际多任务环境应用前景广阔。

Abstract: To teach robots complex manipulation tasks, it is now a common practice to fine-tune a pre-trained vision-language-action model (VLA) on task-specific data. However, since this recipe updates existing representations, it is unsuitable for long-term operation in the real world, where robots must continually adapt to new tasks and environments while retaining the knowledge they have already acquired. Existing continual learning methods for robotics commonly require storing previous data (exemplars), struggle with long task sequences, or rely on task identifiers for deployment. To address these limitations, we propose CLARE, a general, parameter-efficient framework for exemplar-free continual learning with VLAs. CLARE introduces lightweight modular adapters into selected feedforward layers and autonomously expands the model only where necessary when learning a new task, guided by layer-wise feature similarity. During deployment, an autoencoder-based routing mechanism dynamically activates the most relevant adapters without requiring task labels. Through extensive experiments on the LIBERO benchmark, we show that CLARE achieves high performance on new tasks without catastrophic forgetting of earlier tasks, significantly outperforming even exemplar-based methods. Code and data are available at https://tum-lsy.github.io/clare.

</details>


### [161] [Learning Whole-Body Human-Humanoid Interaction from Human-Human Demonstrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09518)
*Wei-Jin Huang,Yue-Yi Zhang,Yi-Lin Wei,Zhi-Wei Xia,Juantao Tan,Yuan-Ming Li,Zhilin Zhao,Wei-Shi Zheng*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新方法，将大量的人与人交互数据有效转换为人形机器人可用的人机交互数据，并通过全新策略大幅提升机器人协作能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于高质量的人—人形机器人交互数据稀缺，研究者希望能利用现有丰富的“人—人”交互数据，提升人形机器人与人类的物理交互能力，但直接转换存在关键联系丢失等问题。

Method: 1）提出了PAIR方法，关注物理接触与语义一致性，将人—人交互数据经过两阶段流程转化为保持接触语义的人机交互数据；2）针对常规模仿学习方法仅能模仿轨迹、缺乏交互理解，设计了D-STAR新策略，将行动的时序（when）和空间（where）分别建模并融合，实现更鲁棒的协作策略学习。

Result: 通过大量仿真实验，证明了PAIR方法生成的数据物理一致性强，D-STAR策略明显优于传统基线，机器人表现出更同步、更具响应性的全身交互。

Conclusion: 整体框架有效填补了高质量HHoI数据不足的难题，大幅提升了人形机器人复杂全身交互学习与实际协作的能力，为未来机器人与人类自然协作奠定了基础。

Abstract: Enabling humanoid robots to physically interact with humans is a critical frontier, but progress is hindered by the scarcity of high-quality Human-Humanoid Interaction (HHoI) data. While leveraging abundant Human-Human Interaction (HHI) data presents a scalable alternative, we first demonstrate that standard retargeting fails by breaking the essential contacts. We address this with PAIR (Physics-Aware Interaction Retargeting), a contact-centric, two-stage pipeline that preserves contact semantics across morphology differences to generate physically consistent HHoI data. This high-quality data, however, exposes a second failure: conventional imitation learning policies merely mimic trajectories and lack interactive understanding. We therefore introduce D-STAR (Decoupled Spatio-Temporal Action Reasoner), a hierarchical policy that disentangles when to act from where to act. In D-STAR, Phase Attention (when) and a Multi-Scale Spatial module (where) are fused by the diffusion head to produce synchronized whole-body behaviors beyond mimicry. By decoupling these reasoning streams, our model learns robust temporal phases without being distracted by spatial noise, leading to responsive, synchronized collaboration. We validate our framework through extensive and rigorous simulations, demonstrating significant performance gains over baseline approaches and a complete, effective pipeline for learning complex whole-body interactions from HHI data.

</details>


### [162] [Multimodal Signal Processing For Thermo-Visible-Lidar Fusion In Real-time 3D Semantic Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.09578)
*Jiajun Sun,Yangyi Ou,Haoyuan Zheng,Chao yang,Yue Ma*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将热成像信息引入三维点云地图的SLAM增强方法，实现了对环境语义的丰富表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统SLAM只关注几何信息，无法满足复杂场景下对热源等特殊语义要素的需求，特别是在灾害评估和工业巡检等需要高温信息的应用场景。

Method: 方法包括：1）对可见光与红外图像进行像素级融合；2）将实时激光雷达点云投影到融合图像流上；3）在热成像通道中分割热源特征，实时识别高温目标；4）将温度信息作为语义层赋予最终3D地图。

Result: 本方法实现了兼具高精度几何与语义（热源）表达的3D地图构建，可在高温目标检测等任务中直接获取语义信息。

Conclusion: 这种融合热成像信息的3D点云语义增强SLAM方法，能够提升复杂环境下机器人的感知能力，在灾害评估和工业维护等领域具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: In complex environments, autonomous robot navigation and environmental perception pose higher requirements for SLAM technology. This paper presents a novel method for semantically enhancing 3D point cloud maps with thermal information. By first performing pixel-level fusion of visible and infrared images, the system projects real-time LiDAR point clouds onto this fused image stream. It then segments heat source features in the thermal channel to instantly identify high temperature targets and applies this temperature information as a semantic layer on the final 3D map. This approach generates maps that not only have accurate geometry but also possess a critical semantic understanding of the environment, making it highly valuable for specific applications like rapid disaster assessment and industrial preventive maintenance.

</details>
